Coin4-doc in Fedora 33

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of Coin4-doc. You might want go back to the main page of Coin4-doc.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-08-01 Fedora Release Engineering - 4.0.0-7 - Second attempt - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_33_Mass_Rebuild
2020-07-27 Fedora Release Engineering - 4.0.0-6 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_33_Mass_Rebuild
2020-01-28 Fedora Release Engineering - 4.0.0-5 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-12-02 Richard Shaw - 4.0.0-4 - Disable building with glx as it causes crashes in FreeCAD on wayland.
2019-09-17 Richard Shaw - 4.0.0-2 - Update spec file per reviewer comments. - Change package name from Coin4 to coin.
2019-09-03 Richard Shaw - 4.0.0-1 - Initial packaging.
